  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_ffa53cfc-a2ab-4db8-9368-0ced31eeeb5c'
      });

<span id="freeTextContainer17301234952740274969"><i>Some things are worth waiting for…</i><br/><br/>Traveling thousands of miles from home to enter college is the only way nineteen-year-old Avery Morgansten can escape what happened at the Halloween party five years ago—an event that forever changed her life. All she needs to do is make it to her classes on time, make sure the bracelet on her left wrist stays in place, not draw any attent</span>
  <span id="freeText17301234952740274969" style="display:none"><i>Some things are worth waiting for…</i><br /><br />Traveling thousands of miles from home to enter college is the only way nineteen-year-old Avery Morgansten can escape what happened at the Halloween party five years ago—an event that forever changed her life. All she needs to do is make it to her classes on time, make sure the bracelet on her left wrist stays in place, not draw any attention to herself, and maybe—please God—make a few friends, because surely that would be a nice change of pace. The one thing she didn’t need and never planned on was capturing the attention of the one guy who could shatter the precarious future she’s building for herself.<br /><br /><i>Some things are worth experiencing…</i><br /><br />Cameron Hamilton is six feet and three inches of swoon-worthy hotness, complete with a pair of striking blue eyes and a remarkable ability to make her want things she believed were irrevocably stolen from her. She knows she needs to stay away from him, but Cam is freaking everywhere, with his charm, his witty banter, and that damn dimple that’s just so… so lickable. Getting involved with him is dangerous, but when ignoring the simmering tension that sparks whenever they are around each other becomes impossible, he brings out a side of her she never knew existed.<br /><br /><i>Some things should never be kept quiet…</i><br /><br />But when Avery starts receiving threatening emails and phone calls forcing her to face a past she wants silenced, she’s has no other choice but to acknowledge that someone is refusing to allow her to let go of that night when everything changed. When the devastating truth comes out, will she resurface this time with one less scar? And can Cam be there to help her or will he be dragged down with her?<br /><br /><i>And some things are worth fighting for…</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="17301234952740274969" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

To be honest, if your daughter has been reading books like this for a while then stopping it now won't make a difference.               <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9016476-xrysa?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9016476-xrysa?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer548657476" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6410268109610743876">After reading this book I dont think that cookies and eggs will be the same for me.<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380411537ra/808566.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Avery</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411537i/808567.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Avery is starting college but all she wants is to start a new life.<br/>Just consider how lucky she is.<br/>She is living next to a <b>HOTTIE.</b><br/><br/><b>Cam</b><br/> <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380409146i/800870._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>They are both attending astronomy and that brings them closer.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380411537ra/808568.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Cam is determined to go out with her so he is asking her everyday but she is always turning him down.<br/><br/><b>"Go out with me Avery."<br/>"No".<br/>"See?She keeps turning me down."<br/>Jacob shook his head <br/>"You're an idiot Avery."</b><br/><br/>He wants to</span>
  <span id="freeText6410268109610743876" style="display:none">After reading this book I dont think that cookies and eggs will be the same for me.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380411537ra/808566.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Avery</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411537i/808567.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Avery is starting college but all she wants is to start a new life.<br>Just consider how lucky she is.<br>She is living next to a <b>HOTTIE.</b><br><br><b>Cam</b><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380409146i/800870._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>They are both attending astronomy and that brings them closer.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380411537ra/808568.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Cam is determined to go out with her so he is asking her everyday but she is always turning him down.<br><br><b>"Go out with me Avery."<br>"No".<br>"See?She keeps turning me down."<br>Jacob shook his head <br>"You're an idiot Avery."</b><br><br>He wants to be close with her so every Sunday he sneaks into her home to make her breakfast.<br>Ususally their breakfast is such a funny time and they are both enjoying it.<br><br><b>“I'm beginning to think cookies is a code word for something else."<br><br>"Maybe it is." He tugged on my bag again as he took a confident step back, forcing me down another step. "And just think about it. If cookie was a code word, whatever it symbolizes, it's been in your mouth, sweetheart.”</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380411537ra/808569.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>As you all understand she fell for him and they finally went on a date.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/611763.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>Cam's kisses</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/513932.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b><br>“Goodnight, Avery.”<br><br>And then he kissed me—kissed me like he’d had right before he’d left the night of our date. Kissed me like he was a man starving for oxygen and I was the only air he needed to breathe. The hand around my neck held me there, raised up on my elbows as his mouth devoured mine. And that was the only word I could use to accurately explained how he kissed me.<br><br>Cam devoured me.”</b><br><br>This book was so funny but both of them were hiding a past.<br><i>A past that they wanted to forget</i>.<br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380411537ra/808570.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It was pretty obvious what happened to Avery and I was very sad because she didnt deserve it.<br><b>No one does.</b><br>It kind of hit me when Cam told her what he did.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380411537ra/808571.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><u>Why I loved Cam</u> :<br>He is charming and hot. He is not your typical jerk but nice and funny.He definitely has panty dropping eyes and he is that guy that you'd be proud to bring home.<br><br><i>What I really loved about him?</i><br><b>His comfidence.</b><br><br><i>" So you guys weren't more than just friends with benefits?"<br>Cam sent me a widening glance. <br>"We hooked up once in a while but like I told you this weekend, I haven't been with anyone since I met you."<br>"I know. It just seemed like she wanted more."<br>"Wouldn't you?"<br>"Geez we really need to work on your confidence"</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380411537ra/808572.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><u>Why I loved Avery</u>:<br>She is sweet and innocent .She isn't clueless , she is smart and knows how to hide her emotions.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380411537ra/808573.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Cam's parents were amazing and funny people.<br><i>“You listen here, woman.” <br>“You can listen to my foot up your ass if you call me woman again.”<i><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380411537ra/808574.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Avery's parents were .....<br><b>"You are lying."<br>"You are ruinning our lives."</b><br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380411537ra/808575.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380411537ra/808576.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>All in all, this was a perfect read for me.<br>This book combined both humor and real life problems.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380411537ra/808577.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></i></i></span>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_691154543" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/691154543" />
    <a title="Emily May" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4622890-emily-may"><img alt="Emily May" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1528390751p2/4622890.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/691154543?book_show_action=true">Aug 10, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Emily May" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Emily May" href="/user/show/4622890-emily-may">Emily May</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4622890-emily-may?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4622890-emily-may?shelf=na-experiment">na-experiment</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4622890-emily-may?shelf=romance">romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer691154543" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11239633078728095951"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380412193i/810513.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><i>I am conducting what I'm shelving as a "New Adult (NA) Experiment". I'm going to work my way through some of the popular New Adult books and see if I can weed out the crap and hopefully find some surprising gems. Here's hoping!</i><br/><br/>I'm almost tempted to just give <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17314430.Wait_for_You__Wait_for_You___1_' title='Wait for You (Wait for You, #1) by J. Lynn' rel='nofollow noopener'>Wait for You</a> 5 stars because I haven't laughed this much at a book since I don't even remember when. I'm laughing while writing this review (there's no one else in the house, so that's kinda creepy I guess) and it's really not funny, to be h</span>
  <span id="freeText11239633078728095951" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380412193i/810513.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>I am conducting what I'm shelving as a "New Adult (NA) Experiment". I'm going to work my way through some of the popular New Adult books and see if I can weed out the crap and hopefully find some surprising gems. Here's hoping!</i><br><br>I'm almost tempted to just give <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17314430.Wait_for_You__Wait_for_You___1_" title="Wait for You (Wait for You, #1) by J. Lynn" rel="nofollow noopener">Wait for You</a> 5 stars because I haven't laughed this much at a book since I don't even remember when. I'm laughing while writing this review (there's no one else in the house, so that's kinda creepy I guess) and it's really not funny, to be honest. I just... can't. This book. And this author. It's too much. On every level. It makes all the usual cheesy mistakes that a NA contemporary romance tends to do, it uses characters I've seen too many times to count - good girl, reformed bad boy, gay best friend, evil slut who wants reformed bad boy - but it also does something that I don't see too often. Something that brought back memories of a book I read a couple of years ago. A book called <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/9680718.Half_Blood__Covenant___1_" title="Half-Blood (Covenant, #1) by Jennifer L. Armentrout" rel="nofollow noopener">Half-Blood</a>. So when I discovered that Ms Lynn is actually the same author using a new name, I couldn't help letting out something halfway between a laugh and a choking sound at the sheer lack of originality in her books.<br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/9680718.Half_Blood__Covenant___1_" title="Half-Blood (Covenant, #1) by Jennifer L. Armentrout" rel="nofollow noopener">Half-Blood</a> is, I don't feel unfair in saying, a complete rip-off of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/345627.Vampire_Academy__Vampire_Academy___1_" title="Vampire Academy (Vampire Academy, #1) by Richelle Mead" rel="nofollow noopener">Vampire Academy</a>. Please, be my guest, read it if you don't believe me. Tell me that you can't spot all the main characters and scenes being regurgitated with different names. Tell me that the whole pure bloods and half bloods thing isn't taken straight out of Mead's work and planted in another. I would not make this claim lightly because it's a serious thing to accuse someone of, more or less, plagiarism. But I believe that's what it is. And plagiarism is not okay. I don't think quite as serious a claim can be laid against <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17314430.Wait_for_You__Wait_for_You___1_" title="Wait for You (Wait for You, #1) by J. Lynn" rel="nofollow noopener">Wait for You</a>, but yet again I see evidence of recycled scenes and characters that tells me on some level, originality has failed to surface in her work once more.<br><br>Avery Morgenstern is a new arrival at a college in a town far away from her home. She enters on her first day and walks (literally) into the hottest guy in school. The reformed badboy/playboy/whatever. Everyone wants him. He could have any girl in their college. And yet, for some reason I have been unable to fathom, he only has eyes for Ms clutzy new girl. They naturally find themselves paired together for a class project (astronomy class - which offers much in the way of star-gazing material). He wants her. She says no because she has issues. She's "not like other girls". Needs saving constantly. Blah-de-blah. I've seen this all in a million different things. I don't think I need to point out the glaringly obvious one...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1439314730ra/15821246.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Oh yeah, and did I mention that she meets him and starts going loopy over his muscles on <b>page 2</b>? And I really wish she wouldn't blush so much. What's with so many YA/NA heroines being so prudish? I'm not talking about Avery's personal issues with sex here (I'll get to those later), it doesn't take anywhere near "sex" to make her blush. I understand it when she walks into Cam (hot dude), I would have blushed in school if I'd walked into the hottest guy there. But I don't understand it when she's talking to her friends and they ask her if she thinks a guy's hot. I would have talked shamelessly with my girlfriends about the hotness of guys at twelve years old, never mind nineteen. <br><br>Some of the things being thought/said in this novel are ridiculous. Hilarious for a while, but ultimately ridiculous. Cam lays it all out straight away with "I'm used to having girls throw themselves at me" and Jacob (flamboyant gay friend) bursts onto the scene with lines like this "I don't want my fine ass to be tainted by sitting on that floor". They're all like caricatures and I can't take a single one of them seriously. I also wish someone would inform romance authors that petnames suck. I don't care if it's sweetheart or sunshine or baby or kitten *vomits* - they all suck and infantilise women in a way that just irritates me.<br><br><b>"Blood drained from my face and rushed to other parts of my body in a really odd and confusing way."</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380432532ra/868885.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>What exactly is odd or confusing about that? Are you twelve?<br><br>Why is this hot: <b>"I'm a lot to handle, but I can assure you, you'll have fun handling me."</b> I've met drunk perverts in bars with better lines than that.<br><br>There's some crazy wish fulfillment thing going on here with Cam. He's one of those obscenely beautiful male figures with an arrogant personality that I assume we're supposed to find sexy (and clearly, from the ratings, many people do). But I just found the lines he came out with either cringy or hilarious. Or both. He walks around shirtless most of the time with his perfect muscles rippling (oh my god, I will not miss the endless descriptions of his perfect muscles). A beautiful woman called Steph spends her time hanging all over him with her breasts bursting out of her clothes, and yet he never notices(!). He says things like "Avery Morgansten, we meet again." *eye roll* "We have to stop meeting like this." *eye roll* And I don't know whether this was, for me, the best or worst bit of the novel:<br><br><b>
  <i>Cam took a bite of his cookie and closed his eyes. A deep sound emanated from his throat - a growl of pleasure. My heart jumped and my cheeks heated even more as I stared at him. He made the sound again, and my mouth dropped open. A row down, a girl turned in her seat, her eyes clouded over.</i>
</b><br><br>I laughed so much. It's a cookie! It's a fucking cookie! *Can't. Breathe. For. Laughing.*<br><br>Most of what I've said so far has been on the funny side of bad but now I'm going to move onto a couple of things that really bugged me. One was the treatment of Steph's character. I know I sound like a broken record and that fact makes me very sad, but I think it's important to keep pointing out the way women are categorised by their sexuality in so many books. The way flirtatious and sexual women who wear revealing clothes are automatically evil and given no further character development. Steph is that character here. She's the one who Cam hooked up with before Avery ever came on the scene, and she's also the one that gets brushed aside like an old rag who can't possibly have any feelings when Cam decides Avery is a special kind of girl who's worth more than being screwed and dumped. It's okay to screw and dump Steph because she's "that kind of girl". This is Avery telling Cam how she's different from Steph:<br><br><b>
  <i>"I'm not like that."<br>"Like what?" he asked.<br>So he was going to make me spell it out. Of course. Why not? "I'm not like her."<br>"I don't just hook up with guys for fun, okay?"</i>
</b><br>Thankfully, Cam calls her out on it. Well, he calls her out on the fact that she doesn't even know the girl she's talking about and so she shouldn't jump to hasty conclusions. Fair point. But then there's also that bit where she shouldn't place girls into categories based on how sexually active they like to be (whether she knows them or not).<br><br>The other thing that really bugged me was when Jacob asked Avery "are you gay?" because she didn't want to have sex with Cam. It really bothered me that someone was made to feel like they had to be attracted to a certain type of guy because he was soooo pretty. And the only other explanation was that she must be gay? Stupid.<br><br>I have one last comment and it's about the dark secret of Avery's past... are we really not supposed to know what's going on? We know she's running away from something. Something a guy called Blaine did to her. Something that makes her have issues with sex and physical contact. Something that made people call her a "whore" and a "liar". Oh, what could it possibly be? Er, no. I can't be the only one who had her "dark secret" pinned from the start, right?<br><br><a href="http://thebookgeek.co.uk" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog</a> | <a href="https://www.leafmarks.com/emilymay" rel="nofollow noopener">Leafmarks</a> | <a href="https://www.facebook.com/thebookgeekreviews" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a> | <a href="https://twitter.com/thebookgeek01" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> | <a href="http://instagram.com/emleemay" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> | <a href="http://mycountryheart.co.uk/" rel="nofollow noopener">Tumblr</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="11239633078728095951" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">

<span id="freeTextContainer7610042848636948378"><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380417388ra/825482.gif' alt='Image Hosted by ImageShack.us' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/><b>“You want to say yes, but you’re just not ready.”<br/>My jaw dropped.<br/>“It’s okay.” His grin turned cocky. “I’m a lot to handle, but I can assure you, you’ll have fun handling me.”<br/><br/><br/><br/>This book =><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380417388ra/825483.gif' alt='Image Hosted by ImageShack.us' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/><br/>A perfect mix of swoony, wonderful, romantic, heartbreaking, angsty, dramatic and beautiful <3 <br/><br/><br/><br/>Me, while reading the book</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380417388ra/825484.gif' alt='Image Hosted by ImageShack.us' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/>From page one, I've had the goofy smile on my face, and my grinning just got bigger and bigger till my cheeks hurt :D <br/>I loved it from star to finish, the romantic parts especially cause I'm a hu</span>
  <span id="freeText7610042848636948378" style="display:none"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380417388ra/825482.gif" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>“You want to say yes, but you’re just not ready.”<br>My jaw dropped.<br>“It’s okay.” His grin turned cocky. “I’m a lot to handle, but I can assure you, you’ll have fun handling me.”<br><br><br><br>This book =&gt;<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380417388ra/825483.gif" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br>A perfect mix of swoony, wonderful, romantic, heartbreaking, angsty, dramatic and beautiful &lt;3 <br><br><br><br>Me, while reading the book</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380417388ra/825484.gif" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>From page one, I've had the goofy smile on my face, and my grinning just got bigger and bigger till my cheeks hurt :D <br>I loved it from star to finish, the romantic parts especially cause I'm a huge romance fan, and I have to admit, even the angsty parts were great, which is a shock cause I don't like them :D<br>One scene got me teary-eyed, and one scene had me gasping in shock and surprise (look at my status below LOL).<br>But yeah, through most of the book I had that look from the gif here :D total dreamy smile &lt;3<br><br><br><br><b>Cam and Avery's first meet</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380417388ra/825485.gif" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>First scene in the book, she's late for class and bumps into him :D<br>He turns on his charm and bam! She's a total goner ahahahahah <br>I kinda loved the book from this scene and just kept on loving it as the book went on :D<br>She kept avoiding him, and he kept flirting with her :D<br>But yeah, this was a total swoon and I like the fact that they met in the first scene and had a billion scenes together, I didn't have to wait half a book for something to happen :D<br><br><br><br><b>Avery</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380417388ra/825486.gif" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>She moved across the country to an unknown university in order to escape her past. <br>Avery is not used to having friends, or being close to someone, because she was pretty much hated in the town she lived in.<br>Lucky, no one knows here here, and she makes new friends, along with Cam, who wants to be more than just friends with her.<br>She never thought she could get attracted to anyone, but with Cam, it all changes. They spend more and more time together, and she can't get him out of her mind, even though she thinks there's nothing there but friendship between them.<br><br><br><br><b>Cameron</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380417388ra/825487.gif" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>From the moment he first sees Avery, he's interested, but he gets that she doesn't want to have anything to do with him. At that moment.<br>Of curse, he isn't lightly discouraged, so he does his best to stay near her, and keeps asking her out even though she constantly refuses him (stupid woman, but oh well).<br>Cam is... pretty much perfect. Maybe a bit too much, but I don't mind :DDD<br>He's gorgeous, smart, confident, funny, he has dark locks of hair that keep falling on his forehead for goodness sake :DD But like I said, I don't really mind :D<br>For one, it's pretty refreshing to read about a guy who knows he's hot and the sh*t ahahaha and he isn't ashamed to say it out loud :D<br>Took me a while to get used to it, but yeah I totally loved him anyway &lt;3<br><br><br><br><b>Their romance</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380417388ra/825488.gif" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>It was so sweet and romantic and swoony! I just totally LOVE it!<br>The cookies, the Sunday breakfast, the stargazing, all the little thingies... *sigh*<br>Even though they were friends, Cam was pretty confident that sooner or later, they'd be together, and he acted accordingly :D <br>Avery, I mean, I admire her for being able to say no to him for such a long time, but I want to kick her for doing it cause seriously??? He's like the perfectest of the perfect (yes I know it's not a word :P), romantic and is willing to wait for her however long it takes &lt;3<br><br><br><br><b>The angsty part of the book</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380417388ra/825489.gif" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Both of the MCs have a secret, something dark in their past that they don't want to share. <br>That's the thing that will bring on the angst and a bit of a separation/fights and all that :((((<br>Here, I felt the most for Cam :((( He was willing to do anything, wait for her no matter how long it took, tell her whatever she wanted to know, and she kept shutting him out :( <br>I just wanted to hug him &lt;3<br>What I didn't expect was her secret. I guessed what it was about and I was half right, but still. Didn't see that angle coming :SSS<br><br><br><br><b>The sex</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380417388ra/825490.gif" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Well, since I haven't read many NA, I can't really say what would be normal or not, but here I was totally surprised by all the smexy times.<br>I mean, it wasn't really explicit or anything, but there were a couple of hot scenes. It was kinda weird, but Ok I guess :DDD<br>I just didn't expect the <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[masturbation, going down oh him and on her, and a couple of sex scenes too. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br>For those of you who want more steam in their YA/NA, this would be a great choice :)))))<br><br><br><br><br><b>Overall<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380417388ra/825491.gif" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>4,5 stars :)<br>I am happy I've read this.<br>I am happy I've started reading this genre all together<br>I am happy I've met Cam because he's definitely re-reading material<br>I just loved this one, and I totally recommend it &lt;3</b><br><br><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer7468461516027017545"><b>1.5 stars</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1436320583ra/15446850.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Drinking game! Every time something cliche happens, take a shot. Warning: alcohol poisoning is a real risk and you should consult your doctor before reading.<br/> <br/><b>Cliche #1</b> <br/><br/>Avery trips on her first day of school and is saved by a cute guy, aka, Cam. He's also kind of a douche. Very shoujo manga-ish.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1436320583ra/15446851.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Cliche #2</b><br/><br/>Avery and Cam are in the same class.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1436320583ra/15446852.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Cliche #3</b><br/><br/>Did I mention they're also partners for a school project?<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1436320583ra/15446853.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Cliche #4</b><br/><br/>And are neighbors in their dorm.<br/><br/><blockquote>
  <i>"I live here."<br/><br/>I gaped at him. The whole h</i></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText7468461516027017545" style="display:none"><b>1.5 stars</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1436320583ra/15446850.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Drinking game! Every time something cliche happens, take a shot. Warning: alcohol poisoning is a real risk and you should consult your doctor before reading.<br> <br><b>Cliche #1</b> <br><br>Avery trips on her first day of school and is saved by a cute guy, aka, Cam. He's also kind of a douche. Very shoujo manga-ish.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1436320583ra/15446851.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Cliche #2</b><br><br>Avery and Cam are in the same class.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1436320583ra/15446852.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Cliche #3</b><br><br>Did I mention they're also partners for a school project?<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1436320583ra/15446853.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Cliche #4</b><br><br>And are neighbors in their dorm.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>"I live here."<br><br>I gaped at him. The whole half naked thing sort of made sense now and I guess so did the tortoise, but it couldn't be. Way too many coincidences."</i>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1436320583ra/15446854.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1436320583ra/15446855.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Cliche #5</b><br><br>Avery is harassed by a guy at a party and Cam pins the guy up against a wall. Just your regular NA damsel-in-distress scenario.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1436320583ra/15446856.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Cliche #6</b><br><br>Slutty mean girl throws herself at Cam every chance she gets.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1436320583ra/15446857.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Cliche #7</b><br><br>Avery gets sick and Cam takes care of her. Changes her shirt, too.<br><br>This genuinely pissed me off. One, because a similar scene happens in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13047090.Onyx" title="Onyx by Jennifer L. Armentrout" rel="nofollow noopener">Onyx</a> and it's just goddamn lazy. <br><br>Two, fucking consent. I don't find it sexy when a girl is feverish and dead to the world and a random guy removes her clothes. Her best friend was there. Even if she is covered in vomit, which we don't know for sure, he should've covered her with a blanket so she doesn't get cold and wait for her best friend to come back and change her. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1436320583ra/15446858.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Cliche #8</b><br><br>Mysterious threatening texts and emails. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Seriously. Molly could've written I was raped by Blaine too in the subject liner and the whole book would done in a hundred pages. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1436320583ra/15446859.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Cliche #9</b><br><br>Cam keeps asking Avery out, even though she denies every time. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>A flush crawled across my cheeks. "I'm not going out with you, Cam."<br><br>"I didn't ask you at this moment, now did I?" One side of his lips curved up. "But you will eventually."</i>
</blockquote><br><br>Because rape culture is hot, yo. If a girl says no, she's just playing hard to get and you should persist. A restraining order is simply a certificate for your efforts.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1436320583ra/15446860.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Cliche #10</b><br><br>Turns out he fell for her <i>because</i> she said no!<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>"I've wanted to be with you since you first turned me down. I've just been waiting for you to come around."</i>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1436320583ra/15446861.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Cliche #11</b><br><br>That fucking crooked smile.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1436320826ra/15446884.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Cliche #12</b><br><br>Cam is sickeningly perfect. <br><br>You know how we're all up in arms over the Maniac Pixie Dream Girl because of John Green's leap in fame. Well, Cam is a Pixie Boy. He's the embodiment of every girl's dream: rippling muscles constantly on display because I assume all his shirts are ripped from chafing against those abs, king of cheesy one-liners, and complete and baffling devotion to our protagonist. <br><br>Ask yourself this, would you go over to a stranger's house, albeit a cute one, every Sunday morning and cook eggs for them? I know I wouldn't. I have assignments, friends, plenty of shit to keep me busy.<br><br>And do not ever underestimate a college student's love of sleep. We would crawl over a mountain of dead kittens for an extra ten minutes.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1436320583ra/15446862.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Cliche #13</b><br><br>Avery's trauma is healed by the magical power of dick.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1431639062ra/14856066.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Final verdict?<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1436320583ra/15446863.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Save a liver. Don't read Wait For You.</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_547724967" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/547724967" />
    <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog"><img alt="Aestas Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1353371225p2/5604583.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/547724967?book_show_action=true">Feb 27, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aestas Book Blog" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog">Aestas Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5604583-aestas-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer547724967" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11156153057710076979"><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411395i/807859._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>4.5 stars -- <b> He had me at sweetheart ♥<br/><br/>This book was JUST what I needed right now!!<br/><br/>I totally understand why everyone is raving about it! I was swooning from the first page and didn’t want to put it down till I finished it. Not to mention that amazing fact that it is a stand-alone!!! A completed romance with a happy ending that leaves you feeling warm and fuzzy. I LOVED IT!! </b><br/><br/>Now, while I fell into insta-love with this book, I very much appreciated that the characters didn’t. I loved that their re</span>
  <span id="freeText11156153057710076979" style="display:none"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411395i/807859._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>4.5 stars -- <b> He had me at sweetheart ♥<br><br>This book was JUST what I needed right now!!<br><br>I totally understand why everyone is raving about it! I was swooning from the first page and didn’t want to put it down till I finished it. Not to mention that amazing fact that it is a stand-alone!!! A completed romance with a happy ending that leaves you feeling warm and fuzzy. I LOVED IT!! </b><br><br>Now, while I fell into insta-love with this book, I very much appreciated that the characters didn’t. I loved that their relationship took time to develop – it was so well paced. After they meet, its actually a little while before they officially become a couple so, as the reader, you get the time to connected with them, laugh over their banter, swoon over them flirting and you get to fall in love with them. And it made it that much more aww-worthy when they did finally get together. Kind of like a reward for you waiting. Again, I loved it!<br><br>K, so what’s the book about?<br><br>The book starts out on the first day of class at University. Avery is rushing, trying not to be late, when she quite literally runs smack into Cam.<br><br><i> <b> Racing up the wide staircase, I barreled through the doubled doors and smacked right into a brick wall…<br>Something strong and hard went around my waist, stopping my free fall…<br>A second later I was pressed against a wall.<br>The wall was strangely warm.<br>The wall chuckled.<br>“Whoa,” a deep voice said. “You okay, sweetheart?” </b></i> <br><br>C’mon… are you not in love already?? Just a wee bit?? I was.<br><br>She finds herself hooked up as astronomy star-gazing partners with this gorgeous swoon guy who bakes her cookies and calls her sweetheart. Seriously, Cam was “gorgeous in all the ways that made girls do stupid things” and very into her but Avery was haunted by scarring events of a fateful night five years ago and was not ready for any sort of relationship. And despite his best efforts at wooing her, she tried to keep her distance romantically, afraid she wouldn’t be able to handle it.<br><br><i> <b> “I don’t want to go out on a date with you.”<br>Cam didn’t look surprised by my response or daunted. “I figured you’d say that.”<br>“Then why did you ask?” …<br>“Because I wanted to.”<br>“Oh. Well. Okay. Glad you got it out of your system.”<br>His brows knitted. “I haven’t gotten it out of my system.”<br>Oh no. “You haven’t?”<br>“Nope” He flashed a charming grin. “There’s always tomorrow.” </b></i> <br><br>But he didn’t give up. He kept asking her. Kept wooing her. Until he finally got through her walls and into her heart.<br><br>I’ll say that there was a point where I got a little frustrated with how much Avery was rejecting him but I kept reminding myself that she was damaged by her past and that she had genuine reasons for her actions. And she really did. I cringed when the truth came out. But I loved that Cam stood by her throughout it all.<br><br><i> <b> “You’re not doing this by yourself. Hell to the mother fucking no.” </b></i> <br><br>The dialogue in this book is just BRILLIANT!! Brilliant brilliant brilliant!! The texting, the banter, the flirting… just pure GOLD! I have SO much of their interactions highlighted in my book. Some are funny, some are sweet, and some are just down right swoon-worthy.<br><br>Cam… seriously. No joke, guys. He is making the fav’s book boyfriend list. He just scored one swoon point after another! I swear, every time he said ‘sweetheart’, my insides would melt. He just had this effortless, magnetic charm that made him impossible not to love. He was thoughtful, flirty, confident, caring…. basically perfect!<br><br><i> <b> “I have so many feels for u.” ♥ ♥ ♥ </b></i> <br><br>And COOKIES!!! I will never again be able to eat cookies without thinking of Cam! **melt** And just in general, I couldn’t stop grinning at all the things he did. MAJOR SWOON POINTS!!!<br><br>The whole book is told from Avery’s POV. I liked her voice and enjoyed her perspective. If I had to make one complaint, it would be that there were a few time jumps (not huge, just like a week here, a few days there) that wasn’t disorienting or anything, but I would have been a bit happier without them. That being said, I still loved the book so really, its all good <br><br>The book reminded me a little of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16113791.The_Coincidence_of_Callie_and_Kayden__The_Coincidence___1_" title="The Coincidence of Callie and Kayden (The Coincidence, #1) by Jessica Sorensen" rel="nofollow noopener">The Coincidence of Callie and Kayden</a>. I think fans of that book will like this and vice versa. But, again, no cliffhanger here!!<br><br><b> There is a happy ending to this book so if you are ever looking for a sweet, funny, touching stand alone with an uberly swoony guy, this would be a great choice! </b><br><br>Definitely recommended!<br><br>4.5 stars<br><br>CASTING<br><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411395i/807860._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411395i/807861._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> For more of my reviews, visit <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Aestas Book Blog</a><br><br>And come join the Aestas Book Blog <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener"> Facebook Page</a></b></span>
  <a data-text-id="11156153057710076979" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer8949446089952742622">Review posted at: <a href='http://sweptawaybyromance.blogspot.com/?m=1' rel='nofollow noopener'> Swept Away By Romance</a> <br/><br/><b>Charming 4 1/2 stars!</b><br/><br/>I very much enjoyed reading this book. It was one of the most endearing, touching, and fun friends-to-lovers tropes I've read in a long time. I adored and swooned over Cam (Oh, how I LOVED him), sympathized with and understood Avery, and felt they shined brilliantly together. <br/><br/>I did feel this book leaned more toward Young Adult in content than New Adult, but that's why it appealed to me. There was a freshness and youthfulness to this b</span>
  <span id="freeText8949446089952742622" style="display:none">Review posted at: <a href="http://sweptawaybyromance.blogspot.com/?m=1" rel="nofollow noopener"> Swept Away By Romance</a> <br /><br /><b>Charming 4 1/2 stars!</b><br /><br />I very much enjoyed reading this book. It was one of the most endearing, touching, and fun friends-to-lovers tropes I've read in a long time. I adored and swooned over Cam (Oh, how I LOVED him), sympathized with and understood Avery, and felt they shined brilliantly together. <br /><br />I did feel this book leaned more toward Young Adult in content than New Adult, but that's why it appealed to me. There was a freshness and youthfulness to this book that I loved. It was refreshing to read a YA/NA plot where I felt the storytelling made sense and was neither manufactured nor contrived to elicit artificial rather than real emotions. I felt everything these characters experienced and I loved it. <br /><br />I had a great time reading <i>Wait for You</i>. This wonderful story overflowed with angst, laugher, and sexual tension. I highly recommend this gem of a story. </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer5900153792043106469">i need to keep reminding myself that if i had read this when it first came out and i had none of JLAs other books to compare it to, i probably would have really enjoyed this more (which is why im rounding up).<br/><br/>because this story definitely feels dated. and some of the storytelling is… a choice. theres some blatant stereotyping going on when it comes to certain characterisation and some of the dialogue is pretty cringey. <br/><br/>but i did enjoy this, for the most part. i liked how cam is a genuinely a goo</span>
  <span id="freeText5900153792043106469" style="display:none">i need to keep reminding myself that if i had read this when it first came out and i had none of JLAs other books to compare it to, i probably would have really enjoyed this more (which is why im rounding up).<br /><br />because this story definitely feels dated. and some of the storytelling is… a choice. theres some blatant stereotyping going on when it comes to certain characterisation and some of the dialogue is pretty cringey. <br /><br />but i did enjoy this, for the most part. i liked how cam is a genuinely a good guy. so many NA books work the bad boy/massive jerk angle, so it was refreshing to have a kind love interest. i also liked that this story is very straightforward. no gimmicks or dramatics - just two people who like each other and work on figuring out their relationship. its sweet. <br /><br />so i will take this for what it is - not quite the best JLA novel out there but still enjoyable.<br /><br /><b>↠ <i>3.5 stars</i></b></span>

<div id="review_547676074" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/547676074" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/547676074?book_show_action=true">Feb 27, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer547676074" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15200457152165936983"><b>5 Stars!</b><br/><br/>Wait For You is one of books that I just couldn’t put down. Once I started, I was a goner. The main reason for that??? This guy-<br/><br/><b>CAM</b><br/><a href='http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/e0f90d29-6aa1-410d-9d91-cd029edc6d44_zps0ac1f677.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411387i/807836.jpg' alt=' photo e0f90d29-6aa1-410d-9d91-cd029edc6d44_zps0ac1f677.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><b>
  <i>Sweet baby Jesus, Blue Eyes was...<br/>He was gorgeous in all the ways that made girls do stupid things.</i>
</b><br/><br/>Wait For You was a story about a girl named   <b>AVERY</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/WaitforyouAvery_zps0ccfba22.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411387i/807837._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo WaitforyouAvery_zps0ccfba22.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><b>
  <i>Whoever came up with the saying you can’t escape your past really knew what they were talking about.</i>
</b><br/><br/>Avery has not had an easy life. She is nineteen years old, and living away from her family. Awa</span>
  <span id="freeText15200457152165936983" style="display:none"><b>5 Stars!</b><br><br>Wait For You is one of books that I just couldn’t put down. Once I started, I was a goner. The main reason for that??? This guy-<br><br><b>CAM</b><br><a href="http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/e0f90d29-6aa1-410d-9d91-cd029edc6d44_zps0ac1f677.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411387i/807836.jpg" alt=" photo e0f90d29-6aa1-410d-9d91-cd029edc6d44_zps0ac1f677.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>
  <i>Sweet baby Jesus, Blue Eyes was...<br>He was gorgeous in all the ways that made girls do stupid things.</i>
</b><br><br>Wait For You was a story about a girl named   <b>AVERY</b><br><br><a href="http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/WaitforyouAvery_zps0ccfba22.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411387i/807837._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo WaitforyouAvery_zps0ccfba22.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>
  <i>Whoever came up with the saying you can’t escape your past really knew what they were talking about.</i>
</b><br><br>Avery has not had an easy life. She is nineteen years old, and living away from her family. Away from the pain of her past, the secrets and things she keeps to herself. She doesn’t really have any friends from home, when she was fourteen years old something traumatic happened to her. It changed everything. She doesn’t let people get close to her, but she has managed to make a few friends while starting at a new school. Jacob and Brit. She still keeps everyone at an arms length. On her first day of classes, she runs into him. Cameron Hamilton.<br><br><b>
  <i>“I’m used to having girls throw themselves at me. Trying to jump on my back is new, though. Kind of liked it.” <br>“I wasn’t trying to jump on your back or throw myself at you.” <br>“You weren’t? Well, that a shame. If so, it would have made this the best first day of class in history.”</i>
</b><br><br>Cam and Avery get paired together in their astronomy class. And she finds out he is her neighbor. He starts turing up everywhere, and it is unnerving for her. Cam and Avery become friends. They hang out, eat breakfast together on Sundays, she has an easy friendship with Cam. Cam wants more from Avery, and he is persistent. He asks her out constantly, and she is constantly turning him down. But there is something about Cam...<br><br><b>Cam was different. He’d always been different.</b><br><br>Eventually, after a lot of flirting and chemistry brewing, Avery decides to say yes to a date. Eventually, she realized Cam means what he says. <br><br><b>“I’ll be available whenever you want me to be.”</b><br><br>For the first time in a long time, Avery feels safe. Loved. Cherished. But she is holding on to her past, her secrets. Cam opens up to her, but there are things she just can’t tell him. One night, he discovers one of her secrets, and she freaks out. She doesn’t realize that Cam still wants her, scars and all.<br><br><a href="http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Waitforyou-scars_zps02d27230.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411387i/807838.jpg" alt=" photo Waitforyou-scars_zps02d27230.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>She spends a while without Cam. Missing him. Lonely. Depressed. Eventually, they work it out. Avery realizes that her heart wants Cam. He is it for her. And he wants her more than anything.<br><br><b>
  <i>“There’s not a single part of you that I don’t want, you understand? I want to be on you and inside of you.”<br><br>“I’m serious about you, Avery. If you want me for real, you have me.”<br> “I want you for real.”</i>
</b><br><br>But she is still holding on to a secret that could tear them apart. How can they make a relationship work when she is unwilling to trust Cam and tell him the truth?<br><br><br>I am going to go start with Cam, because he made the book for me! What a sweet, funny, swoonworthy and sexy guy! He could be a little cocky at times, but I loved him! He is attentive, hot and he bakes! He also says things like this that made me melt <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[
  <b>
    <i>“I have hope because I love you- I’ve been in love with you, Avery. Probably before I even realized I was.”</i>
  </b>
 <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>Cam- you are a new book boyfriend of mine for sure!!!<br>I was happy to see Avery overcome her past at the end of the book. I was glad she confronted her parents and got some of the closure she needed. <br>Tyler was a hilarious character! Loved him!!!<br><i>“Good, because if a guy isn’t making you walk funny after sex, then he probably isn’t anything to write home to mom about.”</i><br><br>An emotional beautiful story about love, trust, overcoming your past, and moving on. A lovely book with a terrific ending! <br><br><b>
  <i>“I want you, Cam.” <br>“You have me,” he groaned. “You so fucking have me.”</i>
</b><br><br><a href="http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/12263063-b2ef-4109-9b80-0a68e14c1096_zps43334fb2.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411387i/807839._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 12263063-b2ef-4109-9b80-0a68e14c1096_zps43334fb2.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="15200457152165936983" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_557906075" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/557906075" />
    <a title="Tough Critic Book Reviews" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5336035-tough-critic-book-reviews"><img alt="Tough Critic Book Reviews" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1345668583p2/5336035.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/557906075?book_show_action=true">Mar 10, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tough Critic Book Reviews" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tough Critic Book Reviews" href="/user/show/5336035-tough-critic-book-reviews">Tough Critic Book Reviews</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer557906075" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13210485611208120663"><b>4.5~stars<br/><br/>Going commando and a spoonful of funfetti icing...</b><br/><br/>First off, I’m extremely mad at you world for not making me read this book sooner. No seriously, WHAT THE HELL!?!? <br/><br/>It seems like lately my life has been nothing, but good books...decent books. Books that are just...okay. I have been drowning, completely submerged in 3~star books. I’ve been sinking faster than the Titanic. <i>Wait for You</i> was my life raft! I’m saved!! ~Cue the hallelujah chorus~<br/><br/>Let me start by twat kicking some of the negati</span>
  <span id="freeText13210485611208120663" style="display:none"><b>4.5~stars<br /><br />Going commando and a spoonful of funfetti icing...</b><br /><br />First off, I’m extremely mad at you world for not making me read this book sooner. No seriously, WHAT THE HELL!?!? <br /><br />It seems like lately my life has been nothing, but good books...decent books. Books that are just...okay. I have been drowning, completely submerged in 3~star books. I’ve been sinking faster than the Titanic. <i>Wait for You</i> was my life raft! I’m saved!! ~Cue the hallelujah chorus~<br /><br />Let me start by twat kicking some of the negative issues people are having with this book. Yes, you figure out Avery’s secret early on, sort of...a little bit. But I don’t think it was suppose to be some big mystery. I think the reader is meant to know, but not <i>know</i>, know...you know?? We know what happened, but not everything. We are given an almost completed puzzle...almost, but there are still pieces missing. Important pieces.<br /><br />The pacing and development of the relationship was perfect!! The buildup, the tension, the wait!! It was real. It was natural. It was perfect. It teased me. It hooked me. It reeled me in. It was the most amazing, <i>amazing</i> relationship foreplay! I couldn’t tell if I was wrapped around the book or the book was wrapped around me. <br /><br />I almost don’t want to write a paragraph about Cam because I may be forced to invent new words. He’s peanut butter dipped in chocolate, a spoonful of funfetti icing, the left over milk after a bowl of cinnamon toast crunch. <i>He</i>, is raw cookie dough. He had me at “Whoa.” The commando scene! The cookie innuendo! Where are my panties?? Where the hell are my panties?? Wham, bam, thank you Cam! <br /><br />Not only did J. Lynn wow me with all things Cam, she showed me the funny. She showed me incredible banter. She showed me intimacy that made me embarrassingly giddy. I’m 31 frickin years old and during the first moment of extreme intimacy she had me burying my face in the bed squealing, kicking my feet, and squealing some more...repeatedly. <br /><br />There were quite a few editing mistakes, but nothing that drew me away from the story. Just enough to make me go, “Huh, wonder where the editor was on that one?” They were easy to overlook, at least for me.<br /><br />I can’t say enough about Cam and Avery's relationship. It was drawn out without dragging on. Cam was perfect, the dialogue was incredible, and the story gave me exactly what I needed, at this moment...right now.<br /><br />READ ON!<br /><br />More at <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.toughcriticbookreviews.blogspot.com">http://www.toughcriticbookreviews.blo...</a><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="13210485611208120663" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_532757945" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/532757945" />
    <a title="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister"><img alt="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1486056026p2/4971692.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/532757945?book_show_action=true">Feb 10, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister" href="/user/show/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister">Kristin (KC) - Traveling Sister</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4971692-kristin-kc---traveling-sister?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer532757945" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16629616906906787460"><b>An extremely sexy, entertaining read!</b><br/><br/>Every aspect of this story was engaging; from the lovable characters to the quirky dialogue and superb writing...I fell head-over-heels in literary love with this story!<br/><br/>Avery Morgansten has a secret—one that has her fleeing to the other side of the country to escape. Her cold-hearted parents are a despicable source of authority and Avery enters her new college completely alone...that is, until her sexy 'run-in' with <b>Cam.</b><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>People got out of the way for C</b></i></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText16629616906906787460" style="display:none"><b>An extremely sexy, entertaining read!</b><br><br>Every aspect of this story was engaging; from the lovable characters to the quirky dialogue and superb writing...I fell head-over-heels in literary love with this story!<br><br>Avery Morgansten has a secret—one that has her fleeing to the other side of the country to escape. Her cold-hearted parents are a despicable source of authority and Avery enters her new college completely alone...that is, until her sexy 'run-in' with <b>Cam.</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>People got out of the way for Cam. He was like a hot Moses, parting the sea of drunk college students.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=sb7xv8" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img height="450" width="300" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380409132i/800845._SY540_.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Cameron Hamilton is perfection! I'm talking top notch, state-of-the-art, book-boyfriend material. He's smart, sexy, funny, confident without being cocky, and adorably patient and understanding. His infamous playboy ways didn't stand a chance against the beautiful and mysterious <b>Avery.</b><br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=n6cni8" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380409132i/800846.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>The build up to Avery and Cam's relationship was a breath of fresh air! Although they had an instant spark, I appreciated the slow and steady, getting-to-know-you process. Avery's tormented past hindered her ability to trust and getting her on a date was no easy task for Cam. But I loved his persistence and their flirtatious banter had me giddy!<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>You've been checking me out, haven't you? In-between your flaming insults? I feel like man candy.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br>This author excels in creating vivid scenes...every situation came alive and felt authentic. The love scenes were tastefully descriptive, sensual, and just flat-out breathtaking. And that first <i>non</i> kiss...<b>wow.</b><br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2w5sg48" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img height="290" width="370" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380409132i/800847.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>But, what I loved most about this story was the connection I felt to its characters. It's so important to care about the fate of these fictional beings, and some stories lack that personal <i>feel</i> that was so strongly present in <i>Wait For You.</i> I truly loved all the main characters, and although Avery held my sympathy and adoration, Cam stole my heart <a href="http://beta.photobucket.com/images/Heart%20gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380222758i/521909.gif" alt="Heart gif photo: heart heart.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><b>Amazing!</b><br><br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2mh7uop" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img height="50" width="50" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380347313i/701667.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><b>
  <u>Book Stats:</u>
</b><br><b>▪	 Genre/Category:</b> Romance/New Adult<br><b>▪	 Steam Caliber:</b> Maximum steam!<br><b>▪ Romance:</b> Slow build-up. Tension-filled. Sexy, sweet connection. <br><b>▪	 Characters:</b> Sweet, adorable, persistent hero. Guarded, damaged, but lovable heroine. <br><b>▪	 Plot:</b> Fun and fresh, with just the right amount of depth and angst. <br><b>▪ Writing:</b> Sexy, engaging, and addictive.<br><b>▪ POV:</b> First person: Heroine <br><b>▪	 Cliffhanger:</b> None<br><b>▪	 Next Installment:</b> Spinoff<br><b>▪ HEA? </b><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Yes <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><a href="http://prettywordsbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412050368i/11316768.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="https://www.facebook.com/pages/Pretty-Words-Book-Blog/860331017317983" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img height='“40"' width="150" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1413062455i/11461733._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_1163090279" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1163090279" />
    <a title="Jessica" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12842423-jessica"><img alt="Jessica" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1539992905p2/12842423.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1163090279?book_show_action=true">Jan 10, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jessica" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jessica" href="/user/show/12842423-jessica">Jessica</a>
      </span>

        rated it
