<div id="review_1011967435" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1011967435" />
    <a title="Ramona Popescu " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/33526516-ramona-popescu"><img alt="Ramona Popescu " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594649997p2/33526516.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1011967435?book_show_action=true">Jul 31, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ramona Popescu " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ramona Popescu " href="/user/show/33526516-ramona-popescu">Ramona Popescu </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/33526516-ramona-popescu?shelf=love-this-series">love-this-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/33526516-ramona-popescu?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/33526516-ramona-popescu?shelf=hot-romance">hot-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1011967435" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8614603075154377632">J.Lynn or Jennifer L. Armentrout is one of the best authors out there right now and by far, the most complex, because she can write almost everything in a flawless manner. Who can actually have 2 pen-names and nail it every single time? Add Jennifer to your list:)<br/><br/>By the name of J.Lynn she developed such an amazing series, with important issues and adorable couple that just stick with you a long time. The first story belongs to Avery and Cam and I know you will love them to death, because Avery’s</span>
  <span id="freeText8614603075154377632" style="display:none">J.Lynn or Jennifer L. Armentrout is one of the best authors out there right now and by far, the most complex, because she can write almost everything in a flawless manner. Who can actually have 2 pen-names and nail it every single time? Add Jennifer to your list:)<br><br>By the name of J.Lynn she developed such an amazing series, with important issues and adorable couple that just stick with you a long time. The first story belongs to Avery and Cam and I know you will love them to death, because Avery’s innocence and Cam’s hotness are hard to forget and bond perfectly to create an amazing story.<br><br>Avery wants to leave behind a traumatic past that hunted her every minute of her life. After being left out by her family, she just wants to start over and maybe one day, forget. Without the love of her parents and true support in dramatic situations, Avery was almost all her life alone. She enters a new college and things will change when she will meet a blue eye boy called Cameron, the star and hottie of all the school. Girls want him and boys want to be him, but Cameron is very laid back and natural with this status. He likes Avery a lot and he feels she is keeping something important. What at the beginning was a puzzle needed to be put together, developed into something more, and slowly, Cam and Avery will fall in love. That love will be questioned by Avery’s demons and inability of letting go, which will challenge their feelings and create a lot of drama for the couple.<br><br>Avery was a great heroine for me and I love her mix of naivety and vulnerability. She was so guarded, but also so eager to feel something new, intense. Even if her chemistry with Cameron was off the charts, she was extremely cautious in having more than a friendship with him, because she was afraid of losing his respect. This element that Jennifer inserted in the book has fantastic but it kind of outraged me in the same time, because no victim of assault or harassment must feel guilty for anything that happened to them. Avery felt dirty and ashamed, this feelings harvested by her family and lack of love.<br><br>Cameron was awesome and one of the best boyfriend from this genre. He was very patient, loving and kind. I liked that the exterior matched the interior and his gentleness towards Avery was heart melting. He knew something was not right with her, and even if there were time when he wanted to find out the truth, he considered that showing Avery how he felt was more important than telling her. This slow burn romance was amazing and Cameron won the gold medal for patience and awesomeness because he managed to pull Avery out of her shell and show her what an amazing girl she is, worthy of love and everything in between.<br><br>This story is very touching, with a great message behind it and I know you will love the couple. A very intense and steamy story, about second chances, loving yourself and taking chances in order to be happy again. Oh and yes, a story about turtles, cookies and astronomy lessons :)<br><br>5 stars!!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1479123324i/21149668._SX540_.png" width="500" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>For more reviews please check <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://readwithloveblog.wordpress.com">https://readwithloveblog.wordpress.com</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="8614603075154377632" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1399325751" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1399325751" />
    <a title="Karlyflower *The Vampire Ninja, Luminescent Monster &amp; Wendigo Nerd Goddess of Canada (according to The Hulk)*" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/17243568-karlyflower-the-vampire-ninja-luminescent-monster-wendigo-nerd-godde"><img alt="Karlyflower *The Vampire Ninja, Luminescent Monster &amp; Wendigo Nerd Goddess of Canada (according to The Hulk)*" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1587623616p2/17243568.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1399325751?book_show_action=true">Sep 23, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Karlyflower *The Vampire Ninja, Luminescent Monster &amp; Wendigo Nerd Goddess of Canada (according to The Hulk)*" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Karlyflower *The Vampire Ninja, Luminescent Monster &amp; Wendigo Nerd Goddess of Canada (according to The Hulk)*" href="/user/show/17243568-karlyflower-the-vampire-ninja-luminescent-monster-wendigo-nerd-godde">Karlyflower *The Vampire Ninja, Luminescent Monster &amp; Wendigo Nerd Goddess of Canada (according to The Hulk)*</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17243568-karlyflower-the-vampire-ninja-luminescent-monster-wendigo-nerd-godde?shelf=buddy-reads">buddy-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17243568-karlyflower-the-vampire-ninja-luminescent-monster-wendigo-nerd-godde?shelf=you-call-this-romance">you-call-this-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17243568-karlyflower-the-vampire-ninja-luminescent-monster-wendigo-nerd-godde?shelf=saved-by-the-penis">saved-by-the-penis</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1399325751" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9528626545799928111">Due to an unfortunate tagging incident and a not-really-but-so-taken challenge on what one *ahem* She-who-is-friends-with-stuffed-dead-animals *ahem* goodreads user might(or might not)read a buddy-read is forthcoming on Friday, November 13th....to include the ab-lovin' aussie, Dino-Jess as well!<br/><br/>The combination of that cover and that blurb make my face muscles twitch:<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1443034529ra/16308838.gif' width='500' height='280' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/><b>The Review</b> (such as it were)<br/><br/><b>2 Stars</b><br/><br/><u>Wait for You</u> is 80% fluffy nothingness and 20% rage-inducing garbage. I have a particular hate </span>
  <span id="freeText9528626545799928111" style="display:none">Due to an unfortunate tagging incident and a not-really-but-so-taken challenge on what one *ahem* She-who-is-friends-with-stuffed-dead-animals *ahem* goodreads user might(or might not)read a buddy-read is forthcoming on Friday, November 13th....to include the ab-lovin' aussie, Dino-Jess as well!<br><br>The combination of that cover and that blurb make my face muscles twitch:<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1443034529ra/16308838.gif" width="500" height="280" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b>The Review</b> (such as it were)<br><br><b>2 Stars</b><br><br><u>Wait for You</u> is 80% fluffy nothingness and 20% rage-inducing garbage. I have a particular hate on for what the lovely Dino-Jess refers to as “Magic Dick Lit”. <br><br>The MC, Avery, is a catastrophic MORON! And while there is a very real part of me that wants to sympathize with her, I just can’t. Gross imbecilic behavior destroys any level of true empathy I could have for her. She walks around in a world of unreality. Monsters are real little girl, and you as much as me should know that. <br><br>On to the love-interest, shall we? Perfect boy * ahem * Cam, is the idiom of one of my biggest issues with the NA genre. Boys like Cam DO NOT EXIST. They just don’t. And while I will concede that sweet boys who bake cookies better than my mom’s mom may exist they certainly do not come wrapped up in faces like Zac Efron’s with bodies like a football linebacker. Give your head a shake. There is no such thing as perfect, and while personally Cam veers a hard left from perfect there is no doubt in my mind that perfection was the goal in mind on his conception. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1447628615ra/17029119.gif" width="500" height="202" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Oh yeah…. I’m sure that boy right there is going to wait months for me to get my own head out of my ass and realize I kind of have a thing for him…. Sure, we’ll go with that * eye roll *. <br><br>As I said 80% of this book is digestible nothingness fluff. It’s cute in the it’s-so-sweet-I-need-a-dentist-on-speed-dial way and I can appreciate that, I can. However, it’s the other 20% that puts my teeth on edge and makes me growl in the base of my throat. No man, no matter how sexy or sweet, will ever heal your trauma. That shit is my single largest issue. You have to face your own demons and wage war on them, no one can do that for you. And while <u>Wait for You</u> is certainly not the worst case of this I’ve ever read it is present and it does make me want to stab a fool. <br><br>I am the last person to say what anyone should or shouldn’t do, it’s just not a vibe I have but man, I hate when serious issues are treated so cavalierly. As plot point rather than the hell they are. I HATE THAT SHIT! <br><br>There is so much after school special used as a plot point in this book. Cam’s “secret” was so transparent and understandable that I cannot even deal. My brother would have done the exact same thing, THE EXACT SAME THING. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ And for the love of whatever deity will listen, that DOES NOT mean he has anger management issues. All it means is he loves his sister. FOR FUCK’S SAKE!  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br>This book’s an overly sweet, contrived mess of bullshit and burying your head in the sand. <b>We are not ostriches. </b><br><br>Incidentally there are also A LOT of grammatical errors and words missed in this story. However, even that was overshadowed by the gross minimizing of real life horrors. I just, I can’t. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1447628615ra/17029120.gif" width="500" height="286" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Thank you for voyaging with me, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1399321646?comment=142897170#comment_142897170" rel="nofollow noopener">Kelly</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1317927321?book_show_action=false&amp;from_review_page=1" rel="nofollow noopener">Dino-Jess</a>!</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="9528626545799928111" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_552551462" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/552551462" />
    <a title="Jen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6049062-jen"><img alt="Jen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1460575899p2/6049062.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/552551462?book_show_action=true">Nov 21, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jen" href="/user/show/6049062-jen">Jen</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17449042-wait-for-you">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer552551462" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10994877584659871449">** 3.5 Stars ***<br/>I have had this series sitting on my Kindle for quite sometime now, and I have set a goal to start some of the older series before the New Year!!! This series is written by J. Lynn...who is also known as Jennifer Armentrout. I have always enjoyed her work, and this book was no exception! I enjoyed it very much, and would have rated it higher if it wasn't for the heroine!!! She put a damper on the story for me, but even still I did enjoy, and can't wait to continue on with this se</span>
  <span id="freeText10994877584659871449" style="display:none">** 3.5 Stars ***<br />I have had this series sitting on my Kindle for quite sometime now, and I have set a goal to start some of the older series before the New Year!!! This series is written by J. Lynn...who is also known as Jennifer Armentrout. I have always enjoyed her work, and this book was no exception! I enjoyed it very much, and would have rated it higher if it wasn't for the heroine!!! She put a damper on the story for me, but even still I did enjoy, and can't wait to continue on with this series<br /><br />Avery moves to Virginia to attend College...she has not friends or family around her, and this is how she prefers it. She left behind a ton of secrets, and doesn't plan on letting anyone know about her past. Unfortunately, her past won't let her be free in more ways than one.<br />In astronomy class, there is a fellow student named Cameron. He is every young womens dream guy, but he only has eyes for the one who would prefer to be left alone!! And believe me when I say, Cam works so hard to get Avery to go on a date with him!!!<br /><br />I adored Cam, he is such a sweetheart, and he stays so loyal to Avery. It really is too bad that Avery has to be such a frustrating heroine with some of her choices she makes. I do understand her issues were certainly valid; but what annoyed me was that it took almost the whole book to come to terms with her trauma. Her lack of trust toward Cameron, made me want to beat her bad!! LOL<br /><br />Over all though, I would recommend this book though. It is book one in the series, and there are six more to go!!! I am very eager to see what other romances are going to blossom through out this series!! I love that this author is always able to make me entertained!!!</span>
  <a data-text-id="10994877584659871449" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('b6Y7L1w7Wup/emK5KnXVuSryMK4RpX6oNrvKTkvTachpjX7/EdwYm4ql9UDjKQ8DWQjJcKgWrVXoTBsI3j6dtA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('t2pk4XEc0nY2f/paVmgQmXsuxCRUN/gXqY+LUYcWjqGxQSExPPuQB8OgbaOfNMojCNQ9+u2EK+p3eFoXEvt63Q==')})
  }

All the rumors yo</span>
  <span id="freeText4734812522167083743" style="display:none">Hey Guys! Please note: I don't send out ARCs for review. If you're interested in reviewing a book of mine before release date, please contact the appropriate publisher. I also do NOT check my Goodreads email.<br /><br />To email me, please use the below addy. <br />jenniferlarmentrout@live.com<br /><br /># 1 New York Times and # 1 International Bestselling author Jennifer lives in Charles Town, West Virginia. All the rumors you’ve heard about her state aren’t true. When she’s not hard at work writing. she spends her time reading, watching really bad zombie movies, pretending to write, hanging out with her husband and her Jack Russell Loki. In early 2015, Jennifer was diagnosed with retinitis pigmentosa, a group of rare genetic disorders that involve a breakdown and death of cells in the retina, eventually resulting in loss of vision, among other complications. Due to this diagnosis, educating people on the varying degrees of blindness has become of passion of hers, right alongside writing, which she plans to do as long as she can. <br /><br />Her dreams of becoming an author started in algebra class, where she spent most of her time writing short stories….which explains her dismal grades in math. Jennifer writes young adult paranormal, science fiction, fantasy, and contemporary romance. She is published with Tor, HarperCollins Avon and William Morrow, Entangled Teen and Brazen, Disney/Hyperion and Harlequin Teen. Her Wicked Series has been optioned by PassionFlix. Jennifer has won numerous awards, including the 2013 Reviewers Choice Award for Wait for You, the 2015 Editor’s Pick for Fall With Me, and the 2014/2015 Moerser-Jugendbuch- Jury award for Obsidian. Her young adult romantic suspense novel DON’T LOOK BACK was a 2014 nominated Best in Young Adult Fiction by YALSA. Her adult romantic suspense novel TILL DEATH was a Amazon Editor’s Pick and iBook Book of the Month. Her young adult contemporary THE PROBLEM WITH FOREVER is a 2017 RITA Award Winner in Young Adult Fiction. She also writes Adult and New Adult contemporary and paranormal romance under the name J. Lynn. She is published by Entangled Brazen and HarperCollins.<br /><br />She is the owner of ApollyCon and The Origin Event, the successful annual events that features over hundred bestselling authors in Young Adult, New Adult, and Adult Fiction, panels, parties, and more.</span>

    first = d.getElementsByTagName('SCRIPT')[0],
    n = load.length,
    i = 0,
    go = function () {
      for (i = 0; i < n; i += 1) {

        script.async = true;
        script.src = load[i];
        first.parentNode.insertBefore(script, first);
      }
    }

    w.attachEvent('onload', go);
  } else {
    w.addEventListener('load', go, false);
